    <td style="text-align: center"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt">The <span id="xdx_906_edei--SecurityExchangeName_c20221213__20221213__us-gaap--StatementClassOfStockAxis__custom--CommonStockParValue.001PerShareMember_zYpXdBB6X9t1"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="From2022-12-132022-12-13_custom_CommonStockParValue.001PerShareMember" format="ixt-sec:exchnameen" name="dei:SecurityExchangeName">Nasdaq</ix:nonNumeric></span> Stock Market LLC</span></td></tr>
  <tr style="vertical-align: top; background-color: White">
    <td style="text-align: center"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><span id="xdx_90C_edei--Security12bTitle_c20221213__20221213__us-gaap--StatementClassOfStockAxis__custom--PreferredSharePurchaseRightMember_zGozPKRNahk3"><ix:nonNumeric contextRef="From2022-12-132022-12-13_custom_PreferredSharePurchaseRightMember" name="dei:Security12bTitle">Preferred Share Purchase Right</ix:nonNumeric></span></span></td>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></p>

<!-- Field: Rule-Page --><div style="margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; width: 100%"><div style="border-top: Black 1pt solid; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid; font-size: 1pt">&#160;</div></div><!-- Field: /Rule-Page -->

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"></p>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1; Options: NewSection; Value: 1 -->
    <div style="border-bottom: Black 1.5pt solid; margin-top: 12pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><p style="margin: 0pt"></p></div>
    <div style="break-before: page; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 12pt"><p style="margin: 0pt">&#160;</p></div>
    <!-- Field: /Page -->

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><b>Item
3.01. <span style="text-decoration: underline">Notice of Delisting or Failure to Satisfy a Continued Listing Rule or Standard; Transfer of Listing.</span></b></span></p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">On December 13, 2022, Rubicon Technology, Inc&#160;(the
&#8220;Company) notified The Nasdaq Stock Market LLC (&#8220;Nasdaq&#8221;) of the Company&#8217;s decision to voluntarily delist its
common stock from the Nasdaq Capital Market and its intent to file a Form 25 with the U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission (the &#8220;SEC&#8221;)
on or about December 23, 2022. As a result, the Company expects the delisting of its common stock to become effective on December 30,
2022.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="margin: 0; font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif"><span style="background-color: white">The Company anticipates that its
common stock will be quoted on the Pink Sheets platform, which is operated by OTC Markets Group Inc.&#160; (the &quot;<b>Pink Sheets</b>&quot;),
and it currently intends to continue to provide information to its stockholders and to take such actions within its control to enable
its common stock to be quoted in the Pink Sheets so that a trading market may continue to exist for its common stock. There is no guarantee,
however, that a broker will continue to make a market in the common stock and that trading of the common stock will continue on the Pink
Sheets or otherwise</span>.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">On October 14, 2022, the Company received notifications from Nasdaq
that it was no longer in compliance with various Nasdaq independent director requirements set forth in Listing Rule 5605. This rule requires,
among other things, that the Company&#8217;s (i) Board of Directors be composed of a majority of independent directors, (ii) Audit Committee
be composed of three independent directors, and (iii) Compensation Committee be composed of two independent directors. The Company&#8217;s
Board of Directors is composed of four directors, one of which is an employee of the Company and therefore is not independent. The Board
has not yet determined whether the two newly appointed directors will be deemed to be independent under the NASDAQ Listing Rules.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify">The Company&#8217;s Board of Directors has determined that the voluntary
delisting of the Company&#8217;s common stock will be in the best interests of the Company and its stockholders. The Board&#8217;s decision
was based on careful review of several factors, including the benefits to the Company of eliminating the expenses of being listed on NASDAQ
and the costs associated with it, as well as eliminating the demands on management&#8217;s time of complying with the Nasdaq listing standards.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item
7.01. <span style="text-decoration: underline">Regulation FD Disclosure</span></b></span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">On December 13, 2022, the
Company issued a press release as required by the Nasdaq listing rules regarding the decision by the Company&#8217;s Board of Directors
to voluntarily delist the Company&#8217;s common stock from the Nasdaq Capital Market. The press release is attached to this Current Report
on Form 8-K as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin-top: 0pt; margin-bottom: 0pt; margin-left: 0in; text-indent: 0in; text-align: justify"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif; font-size: 10pt"><b>Item
9.01.  <span style="text-decoration: underline">Financial Statement and Exhibits</span></b></span></p>
<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1pt; text-align: justify">(d)&#160;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Exhibits.</span><span style="text-decoration: underline"> The
following exhibit index lists the exhibits that are either filed or furnished with this Current Report on Form 8-K.</span></p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1pt; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<BODY STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif">

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: right; background-color: white"><B>Exhibit 99.1</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center; background-color: white">Rubicon Technology Announces
Voluntary Delisting from Nasdaq</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 8pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Bensenville, IL &ndash; December
13, 2022&nbsp;&ndash; Rubicon Technology, Inc. (NASDAQ: RBCN) announced that it has notified&nbsp;The Nasdaq Stock Market LLC&nbsp;(&ldquo;Nasdaq&rdquo;)
of the Company&rsquo;s decision to voluntarily delist its common stock from the Nasdaq Capital Market and its intent to file a Form 25
with the&nbsp;U.S. Securities and Exchange Commission&nbsp;(the &ldquo;SEC&rdquo;) on or about&nbsp;December 23, 2022. As a result, the
Company expects the delisting of its common stock to become effective on December 30, 2022.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white"><FONT STYLE="background-color: white">The
Company anticipates that its common stock will be quoted on the Pink Sheets platform, which is operated by OTC Markets Group Inc.&nbsp;
(the &quot;<B>Pink Sheets</B>&quot;), and it currently intends to continue to provide information to its stockholders and to take such
actions within its control to enable its common stock to be quoted in the Pink Sheets so that a trading market may continue to exist for
its common stock. There is no guarantee, however, that a broker will continue to make a market in the common stock and that trading of
the common stock will continue on the Pink Sheets or otherwise</FONT>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">On October 14, 2022, the
Company received notifications from Nasdaq that it was no longer in compliance with various Nasdaq independent director requirements set
forth in Listing Rule 5605.&nbsp;&nbsp;This rule requires, among other things, that the Company&rsquo;s (i) Board of Directors be composed
of a majority of independent directors, (ii) Audit Committee be composed of three independent directors, and (iii) Compensation Committee
be composed of two independent directors.&nbsp;&nbsp;The Company&rsquo;s Board of Directors is composed of four directors, one of which
is an employee of the Company and therefore is not independent. The Board has not yet determined whether the two newly appointed directors
will be deemed to be independent under the NASDAQ Listing Rules.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">The Company&rsquo;s Board
of Directors has determined that the voluntary delisting of the Company&rsquo;s common stock will be in the best interests of the Company
and its stockholders. The Board&rsquo;s decision was based on careful review of several factors, including the benefits to the Company
of eliminating the expenses of being listed on NASDAQ and the costs associated with it, as well as eliminating the demands on management&rsquo;s
time of complying with the Nasdaq listing standards.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><B>About Rubicon Technology, Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify"><B>&nbsp;</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">Rubicon Technology Worldwide LLC, a wholly owned subsidiary
of RTI, is an advanced materials provider specializing in monocrystalline sapphire products for optical systems and specialty electronic
devices. Rubicon has expertise manufacturing sapphire products with superior quality and precision. Rubicon is ISO 9001 certified and
ITAR registered.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white"><B>Forward-Looking Statements</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">Some statements included
in this news release are forward-looking statements within the meaning of Section&nbsp;27A of the Securities Act of 1933, as amended,
and Section&nbsp;21E of the Exchange Act, and, therefore, involve uncertainties or risks that could cause actual results to differ materially
therefrom.&nbsp;These statements may contain words such as &ldquo;desires,&rdquo; &ldquo;believes,&rdquo; &ldquo;opinion,&rdquo; &ldquo;anticipates,&rdquo;
&ldquo;plans,&rdquo; &ldquo;expects,&rdquo; &ldquo;intends,&rdquo; &ldquo;estimates,&rdquo; &ldquo;seeks,&rdquo; &ldquo;explores&rdquo;
or similar expressions.&nbsp;These statements are not guarantees of the Company&rsquo;s future performance and are subject to risks, uncertainties
and other important factors that could cause actual performance or achievements to differ materially from those expressed or implied by
these forward-looking statements. Additional information regarding factors that could cause results to differ materially from management&rsquo;s
expectations are found in the section entitled &ldquo;Risk Factors&rdquo; in the Company&rsquo;s 2021 Annual Report on Form 10-K&nbsp;filed
with the SEC on March&nbsp;28, 2022, and as amended on April 28, 2022.&nbsp;The Company intends that the forward-looking statements included
herein be subject to the above-mentioned statutory safe harbors. Investors are cautioned not to rely on forward-looking statements.&nbsp;The
Company disclaims any obligation to update forward-looking statements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify; background-color: white">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white"><B>Rubicon Technology, Inc.</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; background-color: white">Timothy E. Brog</P>
